*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01309000

*/*             AND PLACED THE MESSAGE INDEX, TRANSLATED     @Z40LB02*/ 01316000

*/*             THE MESSAGE WILL BE BUILT AND WRITTEN        @Z40LB02*/ 01321000
*/*             TO THE OPERATOR.  IF THE IOSMSG BIT OF       @Z40LB02*/ 01322000
*/*             IOBFLAG3 FIELD IS SET(XCTL TO SYSTEM         @Z40LB02*/ 01323000
*/*             WTO) IT MUST BE SET OFF TO PREVENT TWO       @Z40LB02*/ 01324000
*/*             SENSE DATA MESSAGES FROM BEING PRINTED.      @Z40LB02*/ 01325000

*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01335000

*/*  MODULE NAME = FSMS4678                                  @Z40LB02*/ 01594000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01595000
*/*  DESCRIPTION NAME = FORMAT SENSE MESSAGES 4, 6,7 AND 8   @Z40LB02*/ 01596000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01597000
*/*  FUNCTION = FSMS4678 WILL BUILD THE MESSAGES AND         @Z40LB02*/ 01598000
*/*             ISSUE THE WTO MACRO FOR:                     @Z40LB02*/ 01599000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01600000
*/*             (1) SUBSYSTEM UNIT UNUSABLE MESSAGE          @Z40LB02*/ 01601000
*/*             (2) CARTRIDGE EXIT STATION FULL              @Z40LB02*/ 01602000
*/*             (3) MSC TABLE PACK FAILURE                   @Z40LB02*/ 01603000
*/*             (4) MSC ACCESSOR HAS FAILED                  @Z40LB02*/ 01604000
*/*             (5) STRIPES AVAILABLE ZERO                   @ZA16133*/ 01605000
*/*             (6) TABLE PACK STATUS IF ERROR AT VERIFY     @Z40LB02*/ 01606000
*/*                  TIME                                    @Z40LB02*/ 01607000
*/*             (7) NO DASD SPACE AVAILABLE                  @ZA16133*/ 01608000
*/*             (8) NO TABLE ENTRY SPACE                     @Z40LB02*/ 01609000
*/*             (9) NO FREE CELLS IN MSF                     @Z40LB02*/ 01610000
*/*             (10) UNTHREADABLE CARTRIDGE COND             @ZA16133*/ 01611000
*/*             AND                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01612000
*/*             (11) LAST ONLINE MSS UNIT FAILED             @ZA16133*/ 01613000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01614000
*/*             BEFORE GETTING CONTROL, MAINLINE CODE OF     @Z40LB02*/ 01615000
*/*             THIS MODULE(IGE0301H) WILL HAVE              @Z40LB02*/ 01616000
*/*             COMPLETED THE MESSAGE DETERMINATION PROCESS  @Z40LB02*/ 01617000
*/*             AND PLACED THE MESSAGE INDEX, TRANSLATED     @Z40LB02*/ 01618000
*/*             SENSE, AND  THE ALTERNATE CONSOLE VALUE      @Z40LB02*/ 01619000
*/*             IN THE FORMAT SENSE WORK AREA.               @Z40LB02*/ 01620000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01621000
*/*             THIS THIS ROUTINE(FSMS4678) WILL             @Z40LB02*/ 01622000
*/*             ACCESS PARAMETERS PASSED OM THE FORMAT SENSE @Z40LB02*/ 01623000
*/*             WORK AREA.                                   @Z40LB02*/ 01624000
*/*             IF THE MESSAGE INDEX IS 4, 6, OR 7 THEN      @Z40LB02*/ 01625000
*/*             THE MESSAGE WILL BE BUILT AND WRITTEN        @Z40LB02*/ 01626000
*/*             TO THE OPERATOR.  IF THE IOSMSG BIT OF       @Z40LB02*/ 01627000
*/*             IOBFLAG3 FIELD IS SET(XCTL TO SYSTEM         @Z40LB02*/ 01628000
*/*             WTO) IT MUST BE SET OFF TO PREVENT TWO       @Z40LB02*/ 01629000
*/*             SENSE DATA MESSAGES FROM BEING PRINTED.      @Z40LB02*/ 01630000
*/*             THIS ROUTINE WILL RETURN TO MAINLINE         @Z40LB02*/ 01631000
*/*             CODE TO BUILD AND PRINT SENSE MESSAGE        @Z40LB02*/ 01632000
*/*             AND FOR APPROPRIATE EXIT PROCESSING.         @Z40LB02*/ 01633000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01634000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01635000
*/*  INPUT = REGISTER 1 WILL HAVE ADDRESS OF IOSB.           @Z40LB02*/ 01636000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01637000
*/*  OUTPUT = (1)  REGISTER 1 WILL BE UNCHANGED.             @Z40LB02*/ 01638000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01639000
*/*           (2)  MESSAGES TO THE MASTER CONSOLE BY         @Z40LB02*/ 01640000
*/*           USING SVC 35.                                  @Z40LB02*/ 01641000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01642000
*/*                                                          @Z40LB02*/ 01643000

*/********************************************************************/ 02312000
*/*  MODULE NAME - FSCLNUP                                           */ 02313000
*/*                                                                  */ 02314000
*/*  DESCRIPTIVE NAME - FORMAT SENSE CLEAN UP ROUTINE                */ 02315000
*/*                                                                  */ 02316000
*/*  FUNCTION - THIS SUBROUTINE WILL FREE THE 160 BYTE BLOCK OF      */ 02317000
*/*             STORAGE USED TO BUILD THE MESSAGE.  IN ORDER TO      */ 02318000
*/*             ACCOMPLISH THIS, THE LOCAL LOCK IS OBTAINED TO       */ 02319000
*/*             PROTECT THE FRR STACK.  THE LOCK IS RELEASED AFTER   */ 02320000
*/*             STORAGE AREA IS FREED.                               */ 02321000
*/********************************************************************/ 02322000
*                                                                  0769 02323000
*FSCLNUP:                                                          0769 02324000
*   PROC OPTIONS(NOSAVE,NOSAVEAREA);                               0769 02325000
FSCLNUP  DS    0H                                                  0770 02326000
*   RFY                                                            0770 02327000
*    (REG6,                                                        0770 02328000
*     REG0,                                                        0770 02329000
*     REGF,                                                        0770 02330000
*     BALRREG,                                                     0770 02331000
*     REGB) RSTD;                                                  0770 02332000
*   SAVCLUP=BALRREG;                /* SAVE REGISTER 14      @Z40LB02*/ 02333000
         LR    SAVCLUP,BALRREG                                     0771 02334000
*   GEN REFS(PSALITA);                                             0772 02335000
GETLK1 SETLOCK OBTAIN,TYPE=LOCAL,MODE=UNCOND,                         **02336000
               RELATED=(IECVSMGR,IGE0301H(FREELK1))                     02337000
*   REGD=EWAPTR;                    /* RESTORE REG 13        @Z40LB02*/ 02338000
*                                                                  0773 02339000
         LR    REGD,EWAPTR                                         0773 02340000
*   /*****************************************************************/ 02341000
*   /*                                                               */ 02342000
*   /* NOW THAT THE LOCAL LOCK IS ENGAGED WE CAN FREE THE    @Z40LB02*/ 02343000
*   /* IOS STORAGE AREA USED TO BUILD THE MESSAGE.           @Z40LB02*/ 02344000
*   /* IT IS NECESSARY TO ZERO THE FIRST WORD OF THE 160     @ZA09517*/ 02345000
*   /* BYTE AREA BEING RELEASED.                             @ZA09517*/ 02346000
*   /* REG1=ADDR OF BLOCK TO BE FREED                        @Z40LB02*/ 02347000
*   /* REG11=00000020 TO INDICATE 160 BYTE BLOCK             @Z40LB02*/ 02348000
*   /* REG13=ADDR OF SAVE AREA                               @Z40LB02*/ 02349000
*   /*                                                               */ 02350000
*   /*****************************************************************/ 02351000
*                                                                  0774 02352000
*   FMTSNWA1(1:4)=FMTSNWA1(1:4)&&FMTSNWA1(1:4);/* ZERO WORD  @ZA09517*/ 02353000
         XC    FMTSNWA1(4,FSWAPTR),FMTSNWA1(FSWAPTR)               0774 02354000
*   REGB='00000020'X;                                              0775 02355000
         LA    REGB,32                                             0775 02356000
*   REG0=IOSBPTR;                   /* SAVE REG1, IOSB ADDR@Z40LB02  */ 02357000
         LR    REG0,IOSBPTR                                        0776 02358000
*   IOSBPTR=FSWAPTR;                /* REG1 HAS ADDR OF      @Z40LB02   02359000
*                                      STORAGE AREA          @Z40LB02*/ 02360000

*   REGF=IOCORMGT;                  /* ADDR OF STORAGE MGR   @Z40LB02*/ 02362000
         L     REGF,IOCORMGT(,IOCOMPTR)                            0778 02363000
*   GEN(BAL  BALRREG,4(REGF));      /* FREE STORAGE          @Z40LB02*/ 02364000
         BAL  BALRREG,4(REGF)                                           02365000
*   IOSBPTR=REG0;                   /* RESTORE REG 1         @Z40LB02*/ 02366000
         LR    IOSBPTR,REG0                                        0780 02367000
*   EWAPTR=REGD;                    /* RESTORE REG 13        @Z40LB02*/ 02368000
*                                                                  0781 02369000
         LR    EWAPTR,REGD                                         0781 02370000
*   /*****************************************************************/ 02371000
*   /*                                                               */ 02372000
*   /* FREE LOCAL LOCK GOTTEN FOR STORAGE MANAGER            @Z40LB02*/ 02373000
*   /*                                                               */ 02374000
*   /*****************************************************************/ 02375000
*                                                                  0782 02376000
*   GEN REFS(PSALITA);                                             0782 02377000
FREELK1 SETLOCK RELEASE,TYPE=LOCAL,                                   **02378000
               RELATED=(IECVSMGR,IGE0301H(GETLK1))                      02379000
*   REGC=SAVR12;                                                   0783 02380000

@EF00005 DS    0H                                                  0785 02386000
